# Privacy-Related Changes (Audit Index)

Scope: `rust-v0.105.0-alpha.1` -> `rust-v0.106.0-alpha.5` (30 transitions).

This report is generated from the per-transition `git diff --unified=0` artifacts in this directory.
Inclusion rule: all hunks in privacy-sensitive subsystems are included, plus any other hunks whose text matches the keyword set below.

## Method

- Privacy-sensitive subsystems (all hunks included): `codex-rs/secrets/`, `codex-rs/feedback/`, `codex-rs/network-proxy/`, `codex-rs/otel/`, and selected exact files (approvals, app-server feedback wiring, protocol schema, TUI approval overlay).
- Keyword scan categories:
  - Secrets / Redaction: \bredact\b, \bsanitize\b, \bsanitiz, \bsecret\b, codex-secrets, utils/sanitizer, Authorization, Bearer, cookie
  - Network Controls / Approvals: network_approval, NetworkApproval, network policy, NetworkPolicy, AskForApproval, approval, AcceptAndRemember, Prompt
  - Network Proxy / MITM: \bmitm\b, CONNECT, socks5, http_proxy, proxy, ca\.pem, ca\.key, DNS rebinding, client\.address, server\.address
  - Logging / Tracing / OTEL: \botel\b, OpenTelemetry, tracing, LOG_FORMAT, RUST_LOG, host\.name, histogram, metrics
  - Feedback / Attachments / Upload: feedback/upload, Feedback, upload, attachment, extraLogFiles, rollout\.jsonl
  - Local Paths / UI Replay Safety: LocalImage, local_images, Local file paths, workdir, PathBuf
- For each included hunk: record transition diff file + line number of the `@@` header, the target file path, and the hunk coordinate (`old_range`, `new_range`).

## Executive Summary

- Total included hunks: 3155.
- Categories present: (Uncategorized), Feedback / Attachments / Upload, Local Paths / UI Replay Safety, Logging / Tracing / OTEL, Network Controls / Approvals, Network Proxy / MITM, Secrets / Redaction.

Themes observed in this range (examples link to exact hunks):
- Secrets redaction was consolidated into a dedicated `codex-secrets` crate and reused by other components.
- Network access approvals were reworked to be more structured, and UI presentation was adjusted for network-only approvals.
- Network proxy gained MITM capability for enforcing limited-mode policy on HTTPS CONNECT, and emits more audit/logging around decisions.
- Tracing/OTEL usage expanded (token usage metrics; JSON log format option; host.name resource attribute).
- Feedback upload gained support for attaching extra local log files (increases potential data exposure if used carelessly).
